<div id="review_232822838" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/232822838" />
    <a title="Anna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1632609-anna"><img alt="Anna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1307368032p2/1632609.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/232822838?book_show_action=true">Nov 08, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anna" href="/user/show/1632609-anna">Anna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/5429567-when-will-there-be-good-news">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1632609-anna?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1632609-anna?shelf=mystery-crime">mystery-crime</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1632609-anna?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer232822838" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3503719176899002162">This is the third in the <i>Jackson Brodie</i> series, and is probably my favourite so far.<br/><br/>I adore Jackson. As ever, he’s a magnet for trouble, both personally and professionally; it’s these stumbles, and how he deals with them, which make him so readable, so lovable. He shares this book with would-be lover DCI Louise, teenage girl Reggie, whose determination in adversity is adorable, and tragic childhood survivor Joanna. They, and all their issues and secrets, are brought together to make a thrilling </span>
  <span id="freeText3503719176899002162" style="display:none">This is the third in the <i>Jackson Brodie</i> series, and is probably my favourite so far.<br /><br />I adore Jackson. As ever, he’s a magnet for trouble, both personally and professionally; it’s these stumbles, and how he deals with them, which make him so readable, so lovable. He shares this book with would-be lover DCI Louise, teenage girl Reggie, whose determination in adversity is adorable, and tragic childhood survivor Joanna. They, and all their issues and secrets, are brought together to make a thrilling and poignant mystery/crime story. <br /><br />I love Kate Atkinson’s style. Her characters, main or secondary, are always so well written and believable; the right blend of emotions, flaws and wit. Her storylines are carefully woven, and although they can rely on a string of often crazy coincidences ('coincidences are explanations waiting to happen,' as Jackson would say), they are so well plotted that they fit together perfectly. It’s her wonderfully fleshed-out characters, though, that drive her books, making you <i>feel</i> her stories, rather than just read them.<br /><br />This was a buddy read with my Aussie friends Jemidar and Kim; thanks girls :-)<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3503719176899002162" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('PO+BanMwEaoLgvttq7dlKu37ooYj5cCWUFBk0EEOQTJO3wvKbDvGqAnANXHbXpk4tGgdDcfe79r2eIIuKSvACQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('sm3ARAGV04ozQNouzrtpA6uNzXxzPWFbYidQHXPy8fHAXUrkHp4EiDECFDK+UpUR8h5y95cGThfED7bjG9dwyg==')})
  }
//]]>

Hi<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText6540001554471199273\" style=\"display:none\">Retired detective Cal Hooper moves to a remote village in rural Ireland. His plans are to fix up the dilapidated cottage he\'s bought, to walk the mountains, to put his old police instincts to bed forever.\n\nThen a local boy appeals to him for help. <div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer3863329386087942333">Kate Atkinson was born in York and now lives in Edinburgh. Her first novel, <i>Behind the Scenes at the Museum</i>, won the Whitbread Book of the Year Award and she has been a critically acclaimed international bestselling author ever since.<br/><br/>She is the author of a collection of short stories, <i>Not the End of the World</i>, and of the critically acclaimed novels <i>Human Croquet</i>, <i>Emotionally Weird</i>, <i>Case Histories</i>,</span>
  <span id="freeText3863329386087942333" style="display:none">Kate Atkinson was born in York and now lives in Edinburgh. Her first novel, <i>Behind the Scenes at the Museum</i>, won the Whitbread Book of the Year Award and she has been a critically acclaimed international bestselling author ever since.<br /><br />She is the author of a collection of short stories, <i>Not the End of the World</i>, and of the critically acclaimed novels <i>Human Croquet</i>, <i>Emotionally Weird</i>, <i>Case Histories</i>, and <i>One Good Turn</i>.<br /><br /><i>Case Histories</i> introduced her readers to Jackson Brodie, former police inspector turned private investigator, and won the Saltire Book of the Year Award and the Prix Westminster. <br /><br />When Will There Be Good News? was voted Richard &amp; Judy Book Best Read of the Year. After Case Histories and One Good Turn, it was her third novel to feature the former private detective Jackson Brodie, who makes a welcome return in Started Early, Took My Dog. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3863329386087942333" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
